Ma Xiangbo and Others Petition for Speedy Completion of Unfinished Puhuitang River Project 146

Summer Arrives, and Odors Permeate

Hope for Prompt Dredging to Restore Sanitation

The Puhuitang Dredging Promotion Committee, composed of people from Songjiang and Qingpu counties, chaired by Ma Xiangbo and with committee member Gu Rungui, petitioned the Post-War Rehabilitation Committee of the National Government's Songhu War Zone, requesting them to urge the Municipal Government to instruct the Public Works Bureau to complete the dredging of the sixth district of the Puhuitang River west of Tianyao Bridge in western Shanghai. This area passes through Xujiahui and Tushanwan, with a mix of Chinese and foreign residents and numerous schools. As summer has arrived, this issue is of great importance to the drinking water sanitation of residents and the traffic of boats. Their petition states: "Regarding the matter of petitioning, the Puhuitang River in Songjiang and Qingpu has been reported for dredging for many days. Xiangbo and his colleagues have repeatedly urged the Shanghai section to be completed as soon as possible to comfort the hopes of hundreds of thousands of people along the river. The numerous documents are all in the clear understanding of your council. The former Standing Committee Member Zhang Shouyong and Hu Junzhuang, inspected the river project and also made verbal requests. It was approved to urge the Shanghai Municipal Government to complete the work. However, after nearly a month, the opened ones could not be completed, and the so-called sixth section from Tianyao Bridge to Liu Jing Bridge, which passes through Xujiahui and Tushanwan, with a mix of Chinese and foreign residents and numerous schools, is the most important. Not only has the work not started, but the black water still flows westward without stopping. The people along the river, seeing this situation, are disturbed and tell each other, with many doubts about the Public Works Bureau's plan to complete the river. Now that summer has arrived, the weather is hot, and the odors permeate, which hinders sanitation and endangers lives. Heaven cherishes life, how can we ignore this? Moreover, the sections of Songjiang and Qingpu, from Longgui Nunnery to Jiepai Bridge, have been completed and released, but the water does not flow smoothly. All places near the market towns have turned ochre. Flowing water does not rot, an ancient saying is clear. This not only hinders traffic, but also makes drinking water difficult for residents. Your council holds wisdom and concerns for the people. We implore you to urge the Shanghai Municipal Government to instruct the Public Works Bureau to immediately start work on this sixth section of the undredged river and complete it within a time limit, so that the entire river can flow smoothly, and the people will be grateful, living in harmony and singing praises endlessly. This is truly the blessing of the local area and the good fortune of Xiangbo and others. We present our urgent words, waiting for orders."

Levy of Fisheries Construction Fee 147

Mediation Today

Four fish merchants, Dashengyuan Chang, and others, from the Ice-Fresh Fish Trade Association, as well as Shibu bucket fish merchants, objected to the levy of construction fees by the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang regions, resulting in the confiscation of goods by the Fisheries Administration Bureau. Subsequently, Yu Qiaqing intervened to mediate, fearing that the fresh fish would rot and spoil if left unattended, and allowed the fish to be temporarily returned. It was agreed to discuss the matter further today. According to news from the Fisheries Construction Collection Office, Chen Gongbo, Minister of the Ministry of Industry, believes that Japanese invasion of the Chinese fishery market causes annual losses. To rectify the fishery administration and recover rights, thorough rectification is necessary. However, according to the Fisheries Law, the levy of fishery tax must not exceed 5% of the value. Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Fang Jiaobo, Zhang Shenzhi, Dai Yongtang, Wu Zhenpan, and others opposed this and formed a tax exemption maintenance committee to fight for tax exemption. The Executive Yuan then approved 2% of the value and decided to use the money taken from the fishermen for fishery construction. All previous license fees and miscellaneous taxes were canceled. However, Du and others still believed that this was not enough, as the power was in the hands of the government, and there was concern that the name and reality would not match in the future. Therefore, they petitioned for the establishment of another Fisheries Improvement Committee, with eleven committee members, exceeding the number of fisheries and commercial committee members determined by the Ministry by two. They fought to increase the number to six. The committee established five groups: Economics, Management, Design, Audit, and General Affairs, and began collecting the 2% fisheries construction fee, publicly recommending Dai Yongtang as the director of the collection office. At this time, Director Dai was the Director of General Affairs of the Ice-Fresh Fish Trade Association and reluctantly agreed to take office after being strongly urged. After Director Dai took office, no construction fee was collected. To protect fishermen during the fishing season, he first purchased two patrol ships with advance payments to protect them. After collecting the 1% construction fee, all miscellaneous taxes were canceled. Eight groups of fresh fish merchants and public offices unanimously approved and telegraphed their approval. Previously, with the 1% value, including license fees, each fishing boat had to pay more than 50 yuan. Later, the ocean protection fee was also more than 30 yuan. Now, with the 1% construction fee, if a fishing boat sells goods worth 2,000 yuan, it only needs to pay 20 yuan. Why wouldn't the fishermen be happy? Now, four fish merchants, including Dacheng Yuanchang, and others, in collusion with Shibu bucket fish merchants, are unreasonably objecting, obviously being fooled by a certain country and stirring up trouble. Some unscrupulous merchants are abetting the villains and secretly forming organizations to control and manipulate the situation. The Fisheries Administration Bureau's patrol ship confiscated the fresh fish for non-payment of the construction fee. After mediation by Yu Qiaqing and Fang Jiaobo, the Bureau approved the release, as the fresh fish would rot if left unattended. As for how to make them fully pay the construction fee, Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, Yu Zuoting, and Director Dai will discuss the matter in detail this afternoon at the Ningbo Fellow Association to mediate the matter.

The "Daily News" reports that the Ice-Fresh Fish Trade Association of this city received a notice (No. 41) from the Ham, Salted Fish, and Dried Fish Trade Association of Hangzhou City, stating: "Notice regarding the fisheries construction fee, which our merchants collect on behalf of the government, has been reported to the government and relevant agencies for the record. We have now received instructions from the Provincial Party Department and the Municipal Government, as well as a letter forwarded from the Zhejiang Provincial Chamber of Commerce, stating that the case has been forwarded to the Ministry of Industry for revocation and has been notified to local chambers of commerce and fish merchants. In the future, regarding the construction fee, whether it is ice-fresh or Daqingshan goods, do not pay or collect on behalf of others before the issue is resolved. As the shippers are purely merchants and not fishermen, they have no tax obligations. Therefore, we issue this notice to inform all merchants that they must stop payment as a whole. We issue this notice."

Robbers Use Fake Names to Rent a House and Plunder Extensively 148

The Case Was Solved the Day After the Incident

Bald-Headed Robbers Are Easiest to Identify

Guo Boru, a Cantonese deputy manager of Deldi Real Estate Company at No. 7 Shengping Lane, Zilaihuo Street, French Concession, lives at No. 390 Yuantai Lane, Shandong Road, Public Concession. Because he had spare rooms for rent, he posted rental notices at the front and back doors. On the afternoon of the 3rd of this month, at 1 PM, several robbers knocked on the back door of Guo's house, claiming to rent a house. Guo's maid, Wang Ajin, opened the door and let them in. When these people entered, they claimed to be renting the house to establish a general association. Guo was not at home at the time. His family, hearing the words "general association", expressed their unwillingness to rent the house. At this moment, one of the bald-headed robbers in the group thought that the opportunity should not be missed. He pulled out a handgun and drove everyone in the house to a corner, prohibiting them from making any noise. The remaining robbers entered the rooms, turning over boxes and chests, and plundered extensively for a long time before escaping. Afterward, Guo returned home with the police. Upon inspection, it was found that precious ornaments, clothes, and cash worth approximately 4,661 yuan had been stolen. Guo filed a report with the police, requesting their apprehension. The next day, detectives Tang Jian, Ding Huaguo, Lu Gendi, Zhao Fuhai, and Sun Jishan of the Xinzha Police Station learned that the robbers were having tea upstairs at a Leyuetian Tea House on Nanjing Road. They rushed to search and apprehended three robbers: the bald-headed robber Li Yulin, Zhao Afu, and Liang Shunshun. They found a platinum ring, a diamond ring, a sapphire ring, a gold ring, a gold watch, a gold chain, and 699 yuan in cash on the robbers. They were taken back to the police station. Upon questioning, they revealed that their hideout was Room 23 at the Nanfang Hotel on Jiujiang Road. The Chinese and foreign detectives then rushed to search the room and found another 600 yuan in cash behind the mirror frame hanging on the wall. All of the stolen goods were sent to the First Special District Local Court yesterday morning. Judge Qian Wenji conducted the preliminary hearing. The police lawyer, Li Zhishan, stated the case, and Detective Tang then reported the circumstances of the case in detail, presenting all the recovered stolen goods to the court one by one. The victim, Guo Boru, also brought his maid, Wang Ajin, to the court. Wang identified Li Yulin as the robber holding the handgun, as Li's bald head made him easily recognizable, and stated that Zhao Afu was also one of the robbers present. The judge then questioned the robbers. Only Liang Shunshun denied being a robber. However, as the case required further investigation, the judge ordered the defendants to be remanded in custody for further questioning at a later date.

Follow-Up on the Datong Hotel Blood Case 149

Qiu Dongrong, a 20-year-old Cantonese man, serves as a quartermaster in the Second Battalion of the 364th Regiment of the 183rd Brigade of the 61st Division of the 19th Route Army. He has been married to his wife, Zeng, for many years, but their relationship is not very harmonious. After Qiu left with the army for Fujian, Zeng lived with her in-laws at the Guangtailai Hotel at No. 107 Edward Road (which she owns). However, the relationship between the daughter-in-law and her in-laws was not close, leading to frequent disputes within the family. Recently, Zeng left home because she could no longer endure domestic abuse and sought help from the Women's Association. Qiu Dongrong learned of this and left the army to come to Shanghai. On the afternoon of the 2nd of this month, at 2 PM, he suddenly met Zeng at a friend's house at No. 5 Dade Lane, North Sichuan Road. Upon meeting, the couple was overcome with emotion. Qiu asked her to go to the movies with him, and she agreed. They went out together, and after watching the movie at 5 PM, they went to the Datong Hotel on Yinhua Street and booked Room 517 to stay together. At 7 PM, Qiu left the room, went to Guangtailai, obtained a razor, hid it on his person, and returned to the hotel at 8 PM. The two spent some time together. At 7:30 AM the next morning, as Zeng was fast asleep, Qiu suddenly had a murderous intention. He took out the razor and slashed Zeng's throat. Zeng woke up in extreme pain, resisted, and shouted for help, causing her to be slashed several more times. The tea server heard the commotion and reported it to the Laozha Police Station by telephone. They immediately ordered Detective Huang Yingjie and a foreign detective to go and arrest Qiu. They also took Zeng to the hospital for treatment. As reported in this newspaper, yesterday morning, the police escorted Qiu to the First Special Court Criminal Division. The police lawyer, Ru Baoyi, stated the previous circumstances and stated that he was being prosecuted for premeditated murder under Article 284 of the Criminal Law and should be severely punished according to law. The defendant's lawyer then stated that the court should note that the defendant is an active-duty soldier and should be tried by a military court in accordance with the law before proceeding with the trial. He submitted the symbol and requested a change of date so that evidence could be presented. The police lawyer also agreed. When questioned, Qiu Dongrong stated, "I left the army for Shanghai on February 20 because I was very angry about this family matter. When I came to Shanghai, my superiors knew about it, but I did not ask for leave. On March 1, I received a letter from my superiors approving my resignation." Judge Feng ruled that since the defendant had confessed to leaving the army, he was no longer a soldier, so there was no need for a ruling. As it was getting late, he ordered a change of date for further questioning. The court ordered the forensic doctor to examine Qiu's injuries and verify what happened.

Robbed a Cigarette Paper Store

Wang Wengen, a shop assistant from Ningbo, working for the Qinchang Cigarette Paper Store at No. 52 Wusong Road, was carrying 1,300 yuan in cash to a money shop at No. 136 Ningbo Road at 8:15 AM the day before yesterday to deposit the money. Before the hospital's new regulations are approved and reorganized by the Association, Dr. Wu Jishun will temporarily maintain the status quo in the capacity of the medical director. ㈡ Many donations from various locations have not been collected. It was resolved that the uncollected donations will be handled by the collectors who will contact Secretary Lu of the Association, who will be responsible for collection. ㈢ The Chaozhou Association previously nominated Supervisor Guo Qiming to contact them regarding fundraising, but there has been no concrete response. It was resolved to nominate Zheng Hongnian, Wen Hongen, and Guo Qiming to meet with Chairman Guo Zhongliang and others to have a thorough discussion. ㈣ Wen Zongyao resigned from his position as director some time ago, and no replacement has been appointed. It was resolved to replace him with alternate director Liu Weichi. ㈤ Many fellow villagers in this city and elsewhere have not made donations. It was resolved to nominate directors and supervisors Chen Fengyuan, Chen Qifen, Wu Jiangleng, Wu Jishun, and Mai Zuoheng as fundraising committee members, convened by Director Chen Fengyuan. The meeting adjourned at 8 p.m.

"Comprehensive Compilation of Divination Inscriptions" is a compilation of studies on oracle bone inscriptions, which should be consulted by scholars in China who study this field. It is now sold by the Modern Bookstore on Fourth Malu Road in this city. There are not many books available, so those who wish to purchase should do so quickly.

Free Talk

Want Freedom, Yet Don't Want Freedom 164

— Shujian

In "Free Talk," where we "want freedom," Mr. Qifan is shouting "don't want freedom." His reasons: "Humans fundamentally will not have freedom," "We won't have any freedom," "Limited to a portion of freedom, what's the point of having it?"

But, not having freedom doesn't necessarily mean not having freedom at all, right? For example, don't the Japanese now have the freedom to invade China? Don't capitalist countries have the freedom to destroy goods and products? Don't the unemployed all over the world still have the freedom to starve to death?

Looking at it this way, absolute freedom certainly doesn't exist; but absolute lack of freedom, where would that be?

So, do we still "want freedom"? Or do we "not want freedom"?

If we "want freedom"; then, "do whatever you want." Pushing it to the extreme, I think it will be the same as what Mr. Qifan said, "China is ruined by too much freedom."

If we "don't want freedom"; then, "we must all conform to the rules." Pushing it to the extreme, I think people like Araki and Hitler are hoping we don't want freedom, so they can take the opportunity to rule China.

So, do we still "want freedom"? Or do we "not want freedom"?

My answer is: "Want freedom, yet don't want freedom." That is to say: the freedom we need has two aspects: on the one hand, it is "the freedom of non-freedom"; on the other hand, it is "the non-freedom of freedom."

In "the new society that will appear," everyone knows they are "a member of the community," and everyone is willing to sacrifice individual freedom to complete the freedom of the masses. This is the "freedom of non-freedom" that we need.

In "the new society that will appear," that kind of individual lack of freedom all comes from being willing. That is to say, we need the "non-freedom of freedom."

Thoughts on the Spring and Autumn Society's Public Performance 165

— Yu Dafu

Living in the countryside for a little too long, one naturally picks up the bad habits of loving peace and laziness. In the past two or three years, not only have I been reluctant to step into bustling dance halls and theaters, but even gatherings of celebrities and banquets with friends have rarely interested me. In the days of youthful neurosis, I had an episode of disliking people and being lonely, and now, in my declining middle age, this ailment seems to have returned more powerfully. Recently, I have even started trembling in terror whenever I am among a crowd of people.

On the evening of June 4th, however, as a result of accompanying my nephews and nieces, who had just escaped from Peiping to Shanghai, for a casual stroll, I happened to be in the audience for the first public performance of the Spring and Autumn Society at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association. Although a sorrowful drizzle was falling outside the door, the audience seats were actually sold to about eight or nine out of ten. Looking around, I saw that those sitting there were all middle-class gentlemen with dignified appearances above a certain age. On this point, I felt that the Chinese people had progressed. The general public's view of drama was already different from what it was a dozen years ago, no longer treating it as just a sideshow at school parents' meetings. After seeing the performances on stage (I only watched a segment of the ending of the first play, "Plum Rain," but I watched two acts of the second play, "The Death of a Famous Actor"), the clarity of the dialogue, the naturalness of the actions, and the composure of the characters throughout surprised me at every turn. In these short years, drama has actually greatly progressed, progressing so much that it almost made me shed tears; because China's politics and social conditions have been going backwards step by step in these years with accelerating speed, and only this aspect, this small aspect of drama that has always been looked down upon by people in society, has uniquely and abnormally achieved its great progress!

After being inactive in the countryside for a long time, my connection with art groups has naturally been severed long ago, so I didn't recognize a single familiar face among the audience around me. Because my nephews and nieces were clamoring to go backstage during the intermission, I stepped backstage before leaving the performance venue. I didn't recognize most of the people backstage either. Around these young, enthusiastic fighters, I only saw a spirit of courageously moving forward. The old bad habit of trying hard to imitate the decadent lives of artists from the past has also been dispelled behind the scenes of this new theater group. After briefly greeting a few old acquaintances, I stepped onto the homeward road, shrouded in a gloomy drizzle. Sitting in the car, I was silently thinking, "China still has hope!"

Scenery 166

— Shu Ji

The small ditch meanders like a snake, flowing eastward. To the left of the ditch is a muddy road. Perhaps because the area is sparsely populated, the wheel tracks of wheelbarrows from the spring rain are still piled up there.

The barley is ripe. Under the May sun, the south wind blows, and the ears of barley rise and fall in rows, like the waves of the Huangpu River at dusk. At the edge of the barley field, a cluster of dark wild trees gathers, vaguely sheltering a few dilapidated farmhouses.

On the uneven paths between the fields, an old farmer walks slowly, with a short pipe in his mouth. His tobacco pouch hangs down, swaying in front of his chest with his unsteady steps. As he passes each field, he always bends his already hunched back, plucks an ear of barley, removes the husk, and puts it in his mouth to chew carefully. His face is stiff, without any joyful expression or trace of a wry smile, like a bronze statue that has endured wind and frost for a long time.

Following the paths to the left, for about the distance an arrow can fly, a paddy field cuts off the path. In this dry weather, it only takes a few sunny days for the water in the field to dry up. In one corner of the field, a yellow ox is pulling the wooden wheel of a waterwheel slowly, step by step, seemingly slacking off. He waves his hand absentmindedly and shouts, and the ox arches its back in surprise, raises its tail straight, and quickly quickens its pace, but after pulling less than two laps, it slows down again. He sighs, squats down, and sits on a mound of earth. The gurgling sound of flowing water echoes in the silent air, and he feels very peaceful in his heart.

On the path across the river, a foreigner in hunting clothes walks out, the nickel-plated barrel of his gun flashing in his large palm. A hunting dog follows closely behind him, its nose to the ground, sniffing vigorously.

Suddenly, he crouches down, secretly jumps behind a pile of mounds, and quietly raises his gun. In the dense leaves of a large tree nearby, a turtle dove is hiding.

Bang! A gunshot!

The hunting dog rushes over, but only finds empty space. The turtle dove has already escaped and is standing far away on the frame of the waterwheel. The hunting dog looks back in surprise, watching its master.

The hunter doesn't seem disappointed at all, and stealthily tracks it, then raises his gun again. "Hey!" The farmer sitting on the mound, seeing the hunter's gun pointed at the waterwheel, afraid of hurting his ox, quickly waves his pipe in the air a few times.

The foreigner only glances at him arrogantly, still focusing his gaze on the turtle dove's abdomen.

The farmer becomes even more anxious and rushes over hastily.

At that moment, bang!

The hunting dog bravely rushes across the river. Just as its two front paws grasp the grass roots on the bank, a dark shadow falls in front of it. It rolls over alertly and falls into the water, followed by drops of bright red blood rain from the sky, staining its clean fur.

### Turtle Dove 167

— Zhou Guangxi

It's raining again, and the turtle dove is always calling on the corner of the roof.

It is said that on such rainy days, the turtle dove is not happy to be calling. In fact, its call is lamenting. Every time it's cloudy, it will emit a strange, unbearable odor, and Mrs. Turtle Dove, when she can no longer bear it, has to peck it with her long beak, driving it out of the nest. So when it rains, the turtle dove, suffering from its wife's oppression, has no home to return to and flies in the rain, calling on the corner of the roof. "Coo-coo! Coo-coo!" This is its sad lament!

But who can sympathize with it? On this gloomy rainy day, everyone feels depressed. The rain confines people to their houses, preventing them from seeing friends, and preventing friends from seeing them. So people hate the rain, and even hate the melancholy, annoying calls on the corner of the roof, "Coo-coo! Coo-coo!"

"It's really getting into people's heads," one person says. "If I listen to it any longer, I'll go crazy." Another person says. Yes, who can forgive it for being forced out by its wife to lament? Everyone throws stones at it, and so Mr. Turtle Dove has to swallow his anger and fly elsewhere.

Water flows down from Mr. Turtle Dove's neck and wings. He has to stop on another corner of the roof. He still wants to lament and make the "coo-coo" sound. But being attacked and cursed is his fate, and he is stoned everywhere. No one pities him or sympathizes with him. Such a lament is simply annoying. Whether you were forced out by your wife or not, if you suffer, you are not allowed to cry. You only deserve to close your bird mouth and endure the suffering, flying in the wind and rain until the sky clears!

But when will it clear up? This long, lingering plum rain season!

### Carrot Whiskers 168

— By Julen Kenato, Translated by Lin Qu

Godfather (Continued)

"The most important thing is to wait until your bobber sinks three times before lifting the fishing rod," he said to Carrot Whiskers.

Carrot Whiskers: Why three times?

Godfather: The first time doesn't mean anything: the fish gently nibbles at the hook. The second time, it's no longer a game: the fish swallows the hook. The third time, it's very reliable: the fish can no longer escape. We must never lift it too late.

But Carrot Whiskers liked to fish for river sand fish the most. He took off his shoes, jumped into the water, and stirred the sandy bottom with his feet, making the water muddy. The river sand fish were startled and scurried around, and Carrot Whiskers cast his rod and caught another one. Carrot Whiskers called out to the Godfather, too busy to keep up:

"Sixteen, seventeen, eighteen..."

The Godfather saw that the sun was overhead, so they went back to have lunch together. He desperately stuffed broad beans into Carrot Whiskers' stomach.

"I don't think there's anything better than broad beans," he said to Carrot Whiskers, "but I have to cook them until they're mushy before I eat them. Gnawing on an uncooked broad bean is like chewing a bullet under the wing when eating chicken, making a sound, which is even more uncomfortable than biting on the iron of a pickaxe."

Carrot Whiskers: The broad beans we're eating now melt in your mouth. The broad beans Mom usually cooks aren't very bad. But they're not the same as what we're eating now. She doesn't season the broth well enough.

Godfather: You rascal, I feel so happy watching you eat. I dare say you never ate as much as you could at your mother's.

Carrot Whiskers: It all depends on her appetite. If she's hungry, then I can eat a little more too. Because when she takes some for herself, she gives me a little extra. If she doesn't take any for herself, then I'm done for too.

Godfather: But you can ask her for more, you dummy!

Carrot Whiskers: It's easy to say that, Old Man. I'd rather go hungry than ask her.

Godfather: And me, without children, I'd be willing to let a monkey lick my butt if that monkey was my child! You guys should sort this out.

After the meal, they went all the way to the vineyard. Carrot Whiskers sometimes watched his Godfather work, following closely behind, and sometimes slept on a bunch of grapevines, looking at the sky with some willow buds in his mouth.

Spring Water

Sleeping with the Godfather was something he really dreaded. The room was very cold, and the feather bed was terribly hot. The Godfather's aging limbs felt the warmth of the down, making the boy sweat all over. But he was happy that he could sleep far away from his mother.

"So she scares you to death?" the Godfather asked.

Carrot Whiskers: You'd better say I don't scare her enough. When she wants to teach my brother a lesson, he grabs a broom and stands in front of her without moving. I can swear to you: she stops immediately. Therefore, she prefers to move him with emotion. She says Felix's disposition is so easily moved that people don't need to hit him. Hitting is more suitable for my disposition.

Godfather: You should try taking a broom too, Carrot Whiskers.

Carrot Whiskers: Ah! If only I dared to do it! Felix and I often fight, sometimes playfully, sometimes seriously. I'm as strong as him. I can resist him as well. But if I take a broom to hit Mom, she'll definitely think I'm giving it to her. The broom will fall from my hand into hers, and maybe she'll even say thank you to me before she hits me. (To be continued)

Important News 169

Guangzhou Zhongda Education Research Institute

Hires Italian Scholar to Lecture in China

▲Recently Published Several Series of Books

▲Subsidies for Graduate Students Next Year

The Education Research Institute of National Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou has been established for more than five years and has achieved remarkable results. It is now reported that the Italian government is willing to donate a lectureship, and it has been agreed to hire Professor Xiang Di'er, the first Minister of Education in Mussolini's cabinet, who established the foundation of the new Italian education system, to lecture in China. Professor Xiang Di'er was originally a professor of philosophy at the University of Rome. The philosophy he created has become a school of its own and is highly regarded by scholars in Europe and the United States. He served as Minister of Education for five years, and the current Italian education system can be said to have been created by him. He is currently in charge of compiling the Italian Encyclopedia. Professor Zhuang Zexuan, director of the institute, traveled to Europe last summer and had two in-depth conversations with him. This time, the Italian consul in Hong Kong sent a letter inviting him, and it is expected that he will come to China. In addition to lecturing in Guangzhou, he may also need to give public lectures in other places. It is also reported that among the series of books published by the institute recently, there are "European Secondary Education." Those in printing include "Research on Secondary School Affairs," "Research on Secondary School Libraries and Scientific Equipment," and "European New Education." Three types will be sent to the printer, including "Comparative Theory of Political Education in Various Countries," "The Technology of Studying," and "Historical Teaching in Various Countries." All are published by Minzhi Bookstore. As for Ms. Bao, a British graduate student at the institute, she has completed the investigation of the status of normal education in various provinces, and the materials are being organized. It is heard that the institute plans to recruit five graduate students in Shanghai, Beiping, and other places next year, and each student will be given a subsidy of 600 yuan to encourage them. Application guidelines will be sent upon request.

Yanjing University President Situ Youmei Arrives in Shanghai 170

(Beiping, 6th dispatch) Situ, the president of Peking Yanjing University, specially went to Shanghai from the United States. He has telegraphed Yanjing University that he can return to Beiping on the 15th of this month.

Grand Opening of the Chinese Painting Exhibition Organized by Xu Beihong in France 171

The Chinese painting exhibition organized by Xu Beihong opened in France on May 10th, which can be regarded as the beginning of Chinese art exhibitions in Europe. The French had been eagerly anticipating this event. After Mr. Xu arrived in France, many famous French people went to his home every day to ask to see the paintings, praising them and returning home, competing to publish them in newspapers. At the opening ceremony, the French, from the Minister of Foreign Affairs down to artists and writers, attended in countless numbers. Although it was pouring rain that day, the attendees were extremely crowded. Even the opening of the most important Spring Salon exhibition in France was not so grand. Chinese people, from Minister Gu down, flocked to watch, also gathered together.

The artworks were displayed in six rooms, each room was full, and the doors were almost impassable. Fortunately, the French were very orderly and proceeded in order, otherwise it would have been unimaginable. The Figaro newspaper immediately published the best comments from the world's greatest critics. The French like to use handheld glasses to view paintings, and some even use telescopes. After using the mirrors, they put them down and sat down to watch, observing from near and far, carefully studying each piece for a very long time. As soon as they saw a Chinese person, they shook hands and asked for their name and the author's name, age, and living conditions. Even though the catalog contains detailed information, they are still so concerned. The French know more about painting than the Chinese, and they may not know as much about China as the Chinese do, but they are extremely interested in Chinese painting this time. After watching, they expressed extra respect and warmth for the Chinese. Every time they saw a Chinese person, they said it was very good. They used to be proud, but now they are unusually kind. The painting exhibition has been very successful.

The viewers praised Xu Beihong's paintings very much and competed to meet him. Therefore, Mr. and Mrs. Xu were extremely busy that day, and some were unable to shake hands. News reporters gathered, some photographing the grand occasion, and some photographing Mr. and Mrs. Xu hosting. They were extremely busy. The tense atmosphere of the venue and the importance and kindness shown by the country on the opening day were already like this. Our country has given the foreign country a very good impression. At this time, there are many important French people in Beijing, and the future glory can be expected. The international atmosphere may be better due to this impression. The art promoted by our country with truth, goodness, and beauty is now shining in the world because of this.

▲Discussing the issues of conclusion and reorganization

▲Decided on the date and location of the conference

The Jiangsu Provincial Normal Science Federation held an executive committee meeting at the Provincial Suzhou Women's Normal School a few days ago to discuss issues such as conclusion and reorganization. Zhu Bingheng presided over the meeting, and Lu Shaoji took the minutes. Matters discussed: 1. Conclusion issue. Resolution: The normal independence movement has been completed. This association will hold a conference at Wuxi Normal School at 9:00 am on Saturday, November 11th of the second half of the year to discuss the conclusion method. 2. Issue of publishing the association's work report. (1) Resolved the content of the association's work report and the schools responsible for editing as follows: (1) Association Constitution (Su Women's Normal) (2) Members (Su Women's Normal) (3) Resolutions of previous conferences and executive committee meetings (Su Women's Normal) (4) Work reports of previous sessions (Suzhong Normal Wujiang Township) (5) Exhibition report and education hall orders (Tai Normal Shangzhong Normal) (2) Resolved to collect manuscripts by the end of August and print them in early September. 3. Reorganization issue. Resolution: Submit to the conference for discussion.

Municipal Education Bureau Examination Committee to be Established Soon 173

▲Reports to Begin in Mid-Month

The Municipal Education Bureau previously received an order from the Municipal Government to forward the order from the Examination Yuan to handle the general and higher-level qualification examinations. The bureau immediately decided on the examination dates and submitted them to the Municipal Government for forwarding to the Examination Committee for submission to the Examination Yuan for filing. The details were reported earlier. Now, the bureau believes that the dates of the two examinations are approaching, and the various matters and procedures are complicated and must be handled as soon as possible. It has already sent personnel to prepare in advance. Yesterday, the bureau received an order from the Municipal Government to forward the reply from the Examination Committee. In addition to forwarding the reported examination dates to the Examination Yuan, it has legally requested and been approved to appoint Pan Gongzhan, director of the Municipal Education Bureau, as the chairman of the two examinations. After receiving the order, Director Pan is reportedly following the regulations, selecting and hiring various examination chairmen, and will prepare appointment letters separately for hiring as soon as the chairman's appointment status is received, in order to organize the qualification examination committee and effectively carry out the work. The registration dates for the two items are expected to be in the middle of this month, and the examination dates will be in early next month.

Chinese Speech Competition for Universities in East China 174

▲First Place Goes to Liu Liangzhan for "Fascism Saves China"

▲Jiaotong University Wins the Team Championship with the Most Total Points

English Speech Competition to be Held Today

The Chinese speech competition of the university student speech competition jointly organized by various universities in East China and various universities in Shanghai was held at 3:00 pm yesterday at the Zhenru National Jinan University. The details are recorded as follows:

▲Seven universities participated, with thirteen contestants. The order of speeches and topics are as follows: (1) Zhu Peinong of Jin University spoke on "China's Rural Economy and Rural Revival," (2) Xu Peicong of Zhongda spoke on "Reviving the Countryside and Improving Politics," (3) Gong Shaoxiong of Jiaotong University spoke on "Youthful Maturity," (4) Zhang Guoquan of Jinan University spoke on "Preparing for War," (5) Zhang Zhenhua of Hujiang spoke on "New Paths for Chinese Diplomacy," (6) Shu Zongqiao of Fudan spoke on "University Students and Sex Life," (7) Jiang Tianxun of Fudan spoke on "Resisting Foreign Aggression and Pacifying the Interior," (8) Xia Chengche of Jin University spoke on "Rural Construction and Rural Education," (9) Xu Yanhxian of Zhongda spoke on "The Impact of the US Abolition of the Gold Standard on China," (10) Shen Fudi of Hujiang spoke on "A Glimmer of Hope in Times of Crisis," (11) Liu Liangzhan of Jiaotong University spoke on "Fascism Saves China," (12) Jing Qi of Jinan University spoke on "Analysis and Relief of Chinese National Character," (13) Shen Changhuan of Guanghua spoke on "Blind Person."

▲The competition was held at 3:00 pm in the auditorium of Jinan University, with more than 800 faculty, staff, and students from Jinan University in attendance. Zheng Hongnian was the chairman, Wang Guangyan and Bian Ye Kangxuan Yi were the recorders, Zhang Lie was the master of ceremonies, and Pan Gongzhan, Lin Ke, and Han Yu were the judges. After the rituals, the chairman reported first, and then the competition began. The speaking time for each person was ten minutes. When the time was up, the timekeeper would ring a bell to warn them. The order of speeches was determined by drawing lots. After the speeches were finished at about 5:00 pm, the judges reported the results, and then Mrs. Xi Yushu awarded the prizes and the event ended.

▲The results of the judging are as follows: first place went to Liu Liangzhan of Jiaotong University, second place went to Gong Zhaoxiong of Jiaotong University, third place went to Shu Zongqiao of Fudan, fourth place went to Shen Changhuan of Guanghua, and fifth place went to Shen Fudi (female) of Hujiang. All received prizes. Jiaotong University scored the most points and won the team championship.

▲The prizes awarded included the Wu Mayor Silver Cup for the overall championship, the East China Silver Shield, the Big Education Association Silver Cup (donated by Zhejiang Xingye Bank), the East China Silver Shield (donated by Director Pan), the East China Silver Shield, the Luo Jialun Silver Shield, the Zheng Hongnian Silver Shield for first place, the East China Silver Shield for second place, the East China Silver Shield for third place, the Big Education Association Silver Shield (donated by Guanghua) for fourth place, and the Big Education Association Silver Shield (donated by Hujiang) for fifth place.

▲Zero News from the Venue: The speeches of the representatives of the universities participating in this competition who did not win prizes, such as Jin University, Zhongda, and Jinan University, were also quite remarkable. Liu Liangzhan, who won the first place, had the posture and tone of a foreign orator. Gong Zhaoxiong, who won the second place, and Shu Zongqiao, who won the third place, had novel topics and humorous words, which made the audience laugh through their tears. Shen Changhuan, who won the fourth place, and Shen Fudi, who won the fifth place, spoke pure Mandarin and had clear articulation, which won them a lot of applause from the audience. The prizes for this Big Education Association were all solicited by Xi Yushu separately.

▲The English speech competition will continue today and is scheduled to be held at Jinan University at 1:30 pm today. The participants are still from seven schools, and the judges include Lin Yutang. There are various prizes prepared by the East China Speech and Debate Association and the University Education Association.

Mandarin Society Holds Summer Meeting 175

▲And Decides to Hold Pinyin Competition

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association held its summer quarterly meeting the day before yesterday, with more than ten people including Lu Yiyan and Li Wei'e attending. The motions are recorded as follows: (1) Draft plan for the Pinyin Election Meeting, request for approval (Resolution: The name was changed to Pinyin Competition Meeting, and the plan was approved.) The plan is recorded below. (2) Please publicly recommend drafters of the competition materials for the Pinyin Competition Meeting (It was decided to nominate Li Wei'e, Pei Weisen, and Zu Er three people to draft and submit to the meeting before June 10.) (3) Please decide on the competition points of the Pinyin Competition Meeting for preparation and implementation (Resolution: First contact Shanghai, Nanjing, Wuchang, and Fuzhou, and other places will be carried out successively.) (4) The association should hold a membership solicitation meeting in July this year. Request for public decision whether to proceed as usual (Resolution: During the national crisis, the solicitation of members is temporarily suspended, but those who wish to join this association may be introduced to join by members of this association from July 1st to 30th.) (5) The association should hold a members' representative meeting in August this year. Request for public decision on when to hold it (Resolution: During the national crisis, the meeting is temporarily suspended. The annual meeting expenses shall be published in the summary of this session's affairs. The directors of this association shall be elected by postal voting, with August 20th as the deadline for election.) The Pinyin Competition Meeting plan is as follows: (1) Purpose: This association aims to promote the popularization of Mandarin through Pinyin competitions. (2) Standards: This year's Pinyin competition focuses on accuracy and speed. Pinyin is based on the standard national pronunciation announced by the Ministry of Education. (3) Members: This year's members are limited to students in the third grade of public and private elementary schools above the elementary school. (4) Competition: Number of people: 1. Two students per school (bring their own pencils) 2. Items: Divided into two types: phonetic transcription of Chinese characters and phonetic transcription of Chinese characters. 3. Time: 30 minutes 4. Scoring: Percentage scoring 5. Date: Report and register from 8:00 am on June 25th. The competition starts at 9:00 am 6. Location: Temporarily borrow Shuji Elementary School in Shanghai Tianhou Palace 7. Prizes: Prizes will be awarded to the top five students with the most points in the form of book coupons. The first prize is a book coupon of 10 yuan, the second prize is a book coupon of 5 yuan, the third prize is a book coupon of 3 yuan, the fourth prize is a book coupon of 2 yuan, and the fifth prize is a book coupon of 1 yuan 8. Registration: Participating schools must submit the names, genders, native places, ages, and levels of the participants to the office of the National Mandarin Education Promotion Association in Pingle Li, Xizang Road before June 21st.

Recent News from the Vocational Guidance Center 179

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center is extremely busy as the summer vacation approaches. Various schools have invited Mr. Pan Yangyao, Mr. Yang Chonggao, and others from the center to give lectures on further education and employment. In order to facilitate young people choosing schools for further education, the center has also investigated well-known universities, vocational schools, and normal schools across the country. The investigation covers the content of courses, departments, teachers, graduation requirements, application qualifications and procedures, tuition fees per semester, and the current year's enrollment methods, covering over 150 schools. Additionally, there are about 40 articles written by experts, principals, and teachers providing guidance on further education and employment.

First Sound of the Jiangda Baseball Game 180

Traffic University Victorious Over Fudan University

|Result: 8 to 4|

▲Fudan scored a total of three points in the first four innings.

▲Traffic University scored seven consecutive points in the fifth inning.

Shanghai Chinese baseball, which had been dormant for a long time, saw the Fudan and Traffic Universities compete in the Jiangda Sports Association's baseball special tournament at the China Baseball Field yesterday. This marked the first sound of Chinese baseball, and a detailed account is provided below to whet the readers' appetites and demonstrate the intention to promote the sport.

(Analysis of the Game) Fudan University's strength was considered to be greater. Pitcher Gu Degang had powerful arms and good control, and catcher Li Changfang was also very steady. Fudan won the first four innings with a score of three to zero, assuming they could secure victory. Unexpectedly, in the top of the fifth inning, Fudan's lineup became chaotic and uncontrollable. Pitcher Gu Degang even committed three "four-ball walks", causing Traffic University's morale to suddenly surge, earning them seven consecutive points. Fudan suffered a defeat with a score of four to eight, which was a pity. The lineups of the two teams were as follows:

▲Traffic University Positions▲Fudan University Positions

Liu Youzhang 2nd Base Feng Chaoliang 3rd Base

Li Beiliang Shortstop Jin Zhendong Shortstop

Wen Liandong Center Field Gu Degang Pitcher

Shen Guanlan 1st Base Li Yaohua 1st Base

Wang Changying 3rd Base Wang Shusen Right Field

Gong Yibin Right Field An Bingwu Center Field

Chen Gongxing Left Field Li Changfang Catcher

Shi Shouyi Catcher Wang Zhengyin Left Field

Wu Yingqiong Pitcher Zhou Qiqing 2nd Base

(First Inning)

Fudan started the attack first. The first batter, Feng Chaoliang, hit a single and reached first base. Jin Zhendong struck out. Feng then stole second base. Gu Degang hit a single past first base, and Feng Chaoliang managed to score, earning the first point. Li Yaohua's fly ball was killed by the left fielder. Li Changfang advanced to third base in place of Gu Degang. Wang Shusen went down without success. After the change, Traffic University's Liu Youzhang batted first, but the ball to second base was killed. Li Beiliang's fly ball was caught by the pitcher. Wen Liandong struck out and returned without success. (Fudan 1, Traffic University 0)

(Second Inning)

Traffic University's formation featured a wonderful "double play" performance. After Fudan's An Bingwu wrongly gained a base (due to the opponent's error), Li Changfang powerfully swung his bat, and the ball flew to the left field, where it was cleverly caught by third baseman Wang Changying, and Li was out. An Bingwu, who was on first base, was trying to steal second base when Wang Changying quickly sent the ball to second baseman Liu Youzhang, and An was also killed. Unfortunately, Traffic University's pitcher Wu Yingqiong was disappointing, issuing four walks to Wang Zhengyin. Coupled with the error at second base and the catcher's misthrow, Wang Zhengyin managed to score. Zhou Qiqing went to second base. In the next inning, Traffic University still trailed by one point. After the change, Traffic University's Shen Guanlan struck out, Wang Changying died on a fly ball, Gong Yibin reached base with a "four-ball walk", and Chen Gongxing was at a loss. The second inning ended. (Fudan 1, Traffic University 0)

(Third Inning)

At the beginning of this inning, Traffic University's formation was extremely strict, leaving no gaps to exploit. Fudan's Feng Chaoliang and Gu Degang were both sent out on fly balls. Li Yaohua made a desperate bet, staring intently, and swung his bat fiercely. The ball flew high towards the center field, thinking it would be a "home run", but Traffic University's Wen Liandong aimed it perfectly, rescued Adou, and quickly killed three people, which was extremely easy. After Fudan's formation, Traffic University also made no progress, except for Wu Yingqiong's "four-ball walk" to reach base. (Fudan 0, Traffic University 0)

(Fourth Inning)

Fudan's Wang Shusen reached third base directly due to an error between Traffic University's third and first base, creating a very good opportunity. An Bingwu hit a single and reached first base, returning to home base and adding one point. Li Changfang and Wang Zhengyin did not succeed, so the field was changed. Traffic University's Li Beiliang entered the field and reached first base. Wen Liandong suffered a loss, but due to Li's being killed, he managed to occupy first base. Shen Guanlan struck out, and Wang Changying also failed to make progress. The inning ended. (Fudan 1, Traffic University 0)

(Fifth Inning)

Fudan's three players did not score, and after the change of innings, Traffic University's morale suddenly surged, and their spirits were high. Fudan's pitcher, Gu Degang, on the other hand, changed his usual state, and his pitches were weak. He allowed Gong Yibin to reach base with a "four-ball walk". Chen Gongxing came on and struck a powerful blow, the ball was low and fast, passing through second

base, Gong and Chen each occupied first base. After Shi Shouyi was killed, Wu Yingqiong advanced to first base again, so all three bases were occupied, and the situation was tense. At this time, it was a critical period for the pitcher, and it could not be taken lightly. However, Gu Degang seemed quite anxious due to the cheers of the Traffic University players, and he issued another "four-ball walk" to Liu Youzhang. As a result, Gong Yibin, who was on third base, scored a point without effort. After Li Beiliang's fly ball was out, Traffic University had only one player left. If Fudan could closely monitor, they would not have suffered a major disaster. Who knew that Gu Degang would issue another "four-ball walk"? Wen Liandong also advanced to first base, and Chen Gongxing also scored, gaining two consecutive points. Traffic University was once again full of three bases. As a result, Fudan became more and more flustered, and mistakes piled up. One wrong step caused eternal regret, and Traffic University's momentum became stronger. Later, Shen Guanlan and Wang Changying each performed miraculously, and Gong Yixun even got a "double play". Li Beiliang (running in place of Wu Yingqiong), Liu Youzhang, Wen Liandong, Shen Guanlan, and Wang Changying also returned to score, gaining a total of seven points, defeating Fudan with a score of seven to three. (Fudan 0, Traffic University 7)

(Sixth Inning)

In this inning, Fudan all returned halfway. Wang Shusen reached third base, but was eventually killed and left the field. Traffic University's Shi Shouyi reached base first. Wu Yingqiong struck out. Liu Youzhang's fly ball was caught. Li Beiliang hit a single. Wen Liandong hit the ball, and Shi Shouyi scored, adding one point. The hope of victory became even more consolidated. (Fudan 0, Traffic University 1)

(Seventh Inning)

Fudan's only hope lay in this inning. They proceeded cautiously, hoping to expand their success. However, Traffic University's formation was tight and flawless. Wang Zhengyin and Zhou Zhuqing were out one after another. Feng Chaoliang hit a single, and Jin Zhendong followed. Feng scored, and Gu's hit was ineffective, only gaining one point. As a result, Traffic University reversed the defeat and won with a score of eight to four. (Traffic University did not bat in the bottom half of the inning.) The base umpire was Liu Dacheng, and the ball umpire was Zhou Jiaqi. The scores for each inning were as follows:

Fudan University 1 1 0 1 0 9 1 — 4

Inning Number (1st) (2nd) (3rd) (4th) (5th) (6th) (7th) ——

Traffic University 0 0 0 0 7 1 — 8

French International Tennis Singles Tournament

Crawford Wins Championship 181

Defeats French Ace Cochêt

|British Miss Scriven Wins Women's Championship|

(Paris, 5th) In the French International Tennis Championships, the men's singles final was held. Australian player Crawford defeated French ace Cochêt by a score of 8-6, 6-1, 6-3. Crawford is good at defense. No matter what kind of shot Cochêt used, he was able to handle even the most difficult balls. Crawford also made Cochêt run around, so although Cochêt once led 5-4 and 6-5 in the first set, he was unable to maintain his lead and was defeated by Crawford. This time, the Australian male players, especially Crawford, have caused a strong impression among tennis players. The Australian Tennis Association, unlike what other countries have done, did not hesitate to add new players to the Davis Cup competition team, and their strength is formidable. In the future Davis Cup competition, Japan will definitely eliminate Germany, but when they meet the Australian team between the 17th and 19th of this month, they will definitely be defeated by the Australian players. On the other hand, the British team will definitely win the European final, but it is difficult to know who will win when they meet the Australian team. Also, the women's singles final was held at the same time today, and British player Miss Scriven defeated French Madame 　Diou by a score of 6-2, 4-6, 6-4, and won the championship. Miss Scriven is older and more confident, so she was able to overcome her strong opponent. (Havas Agency)

Next World Games

American Jews Oppose Holding Games in Germany 182

▲Disgust at Germany's Discrimination Against Jews

(New York, 5th, Havas Agency) The American Jewish Congress, due to the discrimination against Jews in Germany, sent a telegram to the American delegation of the Vienna International Olympic Committee, asking them to oppose holding the 1936 Olympic Games in Berlin. Twenty American Olympic athletes also signed the telegram. Previously, the German government intended to transfer the power to prepare for the Olympic Games to the Central Sports Committee, instead of allowing the German Olympic Committee to host it. The International Olympic Committee therefore protested to the German government. There are also rumors that the 1936 Olympic Games may be held in Italy.

Municipal School Teachers and Staff Celebrate Teachers' Day Yesterday 188

▲Present Department of Education Order to Promulgate June 6th as Teachers' Day and Issue Declaration

▲Municipal Middle School Teachers' Union and Hangzhou and Zhenjiang Hold Meetings

|Municipal Elementary Schools|

Yesterday was Teachers' Day. The teachers and staff of the municipal schools in the Nanshi and Zhabei districts of the city held a celebration ceremony at 2 PM at the auditorium of Yangzheng Elementary School in the city, and classes were suspended for half a day in commemoration. Details are recorded below.

▲The participating schools included Xinmin, Junyi, Pengnan, Chaozong, Wanzhu, Wuben, Shangwen, Shihua, Xicheng, Meixi, Danhua, First Experimental Elementary School, Tangwan, Bide, Hean, Xunyu, Nanqu, Gaochang, Nongtan, Nanxun, Feihong, 　Bridge, Haishan, Minglun, Longde, Chengzhi, Zhongdao, Cangqi, Qimei, Jiangjing, Dongming, Chongzheng, Quanzhang, Zhangtang, Jingye, Yongxing, Juyuan, Junpu, and other more than 40 schools, with more than 500 male and female teachers and staff, as well as Superintendent Zeng Shengyuan of the Municipal Education Bureau, Shu Xincheng of China Bookstore, Principal Zheng Xigu of Provincial Industrial High School, and President Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University.

▲Celebration Situation: The meeting started at 2 PM. The presidium included Zhang Yongchun of the First Experimental Elementary School, Qian Xuanqing of Yangzheng, and Zhao Luqing of Xicheng. The master of ceremonies was Xu Yuchang of Bide, and the recorders were Xu Huizhi of Xicheng and Shi Baihu of Yangzheng. The receptionists were Hu Huaitian, Kong Yimin, Zhang Xiaotian, and Jiang Menglin. The entertainment organizers were Yang Songyu and Qian Cijiu. After performing the rituals, Chairman Zhang Yongchun of the presidium gave a report. Superintendent Zeng Shengyuan of the Education Bureau, Shu Xincheng of China Bookstore, Principal Zheng Xigu of Provincial Shanghai High School, Liu Zhanen of Shanghai University, Hu Huaitian, Xu Guanguang, and Chen Pinyi gave speeches in succession. Next, teachers and children from various schools performed entertainment programs. Finally, proposals were discussed, photos were taken, and the meeting adjourned. At 7 PM, a dinner was held at Dafugui to promote fellowship.

▲Chairman's Report: Chairman Zhang Yongchun of the presidium reported that the celebration meeting was initially initiated by more than 20 teachers at the first preparatory meeting on June 1st. The second preparatory meeting was held the next day, setting the location, time, and ceremony for the celebration, and deciding to hold it today. Zhang Yongchun mentioned a few points that were worth noting about the celebration meeting: (1) The issue of the name of Teachers' Day. Strictly speaking, the term "teacher" seems to be limited to elementary school teachers. In fact, when Teachers' Day first started, university professors, middle school teachers, elementary school teachers, and educational administrators all participated. But why not call it Professors' Day or Teachers' Day, but insist on calling it Teachers' Day? It is precisely because elementary education is basic education, and elementary school teachers bear an extremely important responsibility. (2) The origin of Teachers' Day. In 1931, educator Cheng Qibao and others felt the need for teachers to have organizations and connections, so they initiated Teachers' Day. At that time, the Central Party Headquarters, the Ministry of Education, and other departments sent personnel to participate, but June 6th was not promulgated as Teachers' Day. Therefore, when discussing the proposal today, it was decided to formally request the Ministry of Education to issue an official order to promulgate June 6th as Teachers' Day. (3) The goal of Teachers' Day is to improve treatment, guarantee status, and enhance self-cultivation. The methods to achieve this goal seem to require careful consideration.

▲Summary of Speeches (1) Superintendent Zeng Shengyuan of the Municipal Education Bureau gave a speech, stating that past education could not adapt to the education of the present era. Education in the present era should focus on production education, and special attention should be paid to the national consciousness in elementary education. (2) Shu Xincheng's speech was divided into three points: 1. If economic problems cannot be solved, educational treatment will not be easy to improve. 2. If political problems are not on track, the status of education cannot be guaranteed. 3. Before treatment and guarantees are properly resolved, self-cultivation cannot be realized. Therefore, to improve the treatment and status of teachers, it is not something that education itself can solve. Education cannot be separated from society and exist independently. Improving society is the way to improve education. Therefore, teachers themselves should first enrich their knowledge and improve society. (3) Zheng Xigu's speech stated that: 1. The reason why education cannot be improved is that the educational economy cannot be determined. Therefore, determining educational funding is the most important issue. 2. Teachers should be professionalized and take education as a lifelong career. 3. The instability of Chinese teachers' lives has become a common phenomenon. To improve education, we must first seek to stabilize teachers' lives. National teachers should determine the minimum living standard and implement a single-level salary system, and compulsory group savings should be implemented. 4. Restore the inherent status of teachers, and the municipal education community should work together to realize it. (4) Liu Zhanen's speech stated that: 1. Teachers should have a positive spirit to seek the welfare of the country. 2. Teachers should have a spirit of practice and unite together. 3. Teachers should have a spirit of sacrifice to maintain 　　and maintain the country. Hu Huaitian and others also gave speeches, which are omitted here.

▲Entertainment Programs A. Children's Programs: 1. Welcome Song (Yangzheng), 2. Celebration Dance (Shangwen), 3. Harmonica (Feihong), 4. Student Dance (Wanzhu), 5. Singing Game (Danhua), 6. Solo (Wuben), 7. Piccolo Solo (Meixi), 8. Harmonica (Meixi) B. (Teacher Programs) 1. Music (Changmen Complaint, Liu Chunlai), Xicheng, 2. Huqin Solo (Moonlit Night), Wanzhu, 4. ▲Proposals Passed 1. Pass the General Assembly Declaration. 2. Request the Ministry of Education to issue an official order to promulgate June 6th as Teachers' Day and its commemorative measures. 3. Telegraph in support of the Ministry of Education's collection of inheritance tax to be used as educational funding. 4. Request the Gengzi Indemnity Committee to use the surplus profits from Gengzi funds to provide educational funding. 5. Organize the Municipal School Teachers' Amateur Sports Meeting. 6. Organize the Municipal School Teachers' Reading Club. 7. Organize the Joint Association of Municipal School Teachers in the Shanghai Nanshi and Zhabei Districts.

▲General Assembly Declaration: We are the teachers of children, we are the teachers of children in Shanghai. The schools, organizations, equipment, school buildings, environment, etc. where we work may not all be the same, but we all serve the education community of Shanghai. The work, grade level, degree, subject, time, etc. that we engage in may not all be the same, but we all seek the happiness of children in Shanghai. Because of our common goals and intentions, on this day of commemorating Teachers' Day, we have a need to propose several points for discussion with teachers across the country. Teachers' Day is a special day for our teachers, and we should promote and publicize it, and everyone should take this opportunity to celebrate it in a grand and lively way. However, is it enough to just have a lively decoration? In the past two or three years, the Teachers' Day movement has only been the voice of weak teachers and the fragmented expressions of sympathy from teachers, and there have been no concrete and definite commemorative measures. This is the issue of commemorating Teachers' Day, and it is the first point to be proposed for discussion with teachers across the country. "Unity creates strength" and "Unite to start something" are words we often use to tell children. However, how many teachers' organizations are there in various places, and how many organizations are complete and detailed? Some people say, "We organize the teachers' and staff union, nothing more than to fight for guarantees." May I ask, in addition to the issue of guarantees, do we not have other issues that need to be discussed and researched together? If there are issues to be discussed and researched, is there no need for a union organization? Do these need to be proven with facts? This is the issue of whether or not there should be a teachers' and staff union and what attitude the teachers' and staff union should take, and it is the second point to be proposed for discussion with teachers across the country. The world is constantly progressing, and academic inventions are constantly being made. If we do not continue to cultivate ourselves and study, our thinking and views will inevitably lag behind. Especially in today's China, production science is lagging behind everywhere. If we do not catch up, how can we improve the international status of our motherland? To cultivate ourselves and study, what kind of method should we adopt? How can we make it a reality and not just empty talk? This is the issue of the self-improvement of our teachers, and it is the third point to be proposed for discussion with teachers across the country. Scientific inventions have made human life more complex day by day. Our teachers, who are in a position to lead children everywhere, do not need to seek to be superior in everything in terms of enjoying modern civilization, but they should also maintain a position above the horizontal line. This is the issue of improving the welfare of teachers themselves. During the national crisis, everyone should endure hardship. It is difficult to improve, and it is not easy to maintain. What kind of living standard should teachers take? This is the fourth point to be proposed for discussion with teachers across the country. The above issues are directly related to our teachers, and they are the more important of the directly related issues. How should our teachers across the country strive to encourage themselves, so that each issue can be adequately resolved, to increase the vitality of our education community, to increase the interest of our teachers, so that the education community can open up a new situation and have a new way out?

▲Teachers' Dinner: At 7 PM, a dinner was held at Dafugui, and more than 200 teachers and staff attended. Director Pan rushed over from Jinan University and gave a speech on the spot, mentioning three points: (1) The relationship between teachers and students now is not as strong as it was in the old private school era. Now, on the occasion of Teachers' Day, we should find ways to restore and enhance the relationship between teachers and students, and make people in society respect teachers. (2) Just now I heard the chairman report that many resolutions were made at today's commemorative meeting, such as organizing a reading club, which is very valuable. There are too many bad environments for children now. The effect of education is fleeting. If we can actively promote good education in terms of children's reading materials, movies, and broadcasting, and break through the line of defense against bad environments, it is truly an urgent task for teachers at present. (3) Teachers' and staff groups should expand their organizations and do valuable work, which is also very necessary. Please allow me to raise a glass to wish you all the best.

Chronicles of Spring and Autumn

Watching Dragon Boats Beside the Worry-Free Temple 192

— Zhan Lu

The grand dragon boat races I had only heard of but never seen. The dragon boat rowing in both the northern and southern canals has various names: "blocking head oar," "making victory meeting," and "emerging water ascending head," all passed down from the elders. These grand events were before the Taiping Rebellion; back then, resources were abundant, and people did not see war. By the Dragon Boat Festival, the common people naturally had the chance to witness such spectacles. Now, with the economy sluggish and the national crisis severe, even the Dragon Boat Festival is being eliminated, let alone dragon boats? It seems we are not destined to witness such sights.

Some say that while the Dragon Boat Festival can be eliminated, dragon boats should be promoted. Although they are a form of entertainment, they contain the spirit of water sports. I say: that's right, haven't you seen Guangzhou playing dragon boats on a grand scale? I saw recent Cantonese newspapers reporting on dragon boats, and it felt as if I could hear the sound of gongs and drums between the lines. On that day, everyone in the city emptied their houses to watch the dragon boats. The most bustling places, such as Lizhi Bay in the western suburbs and the banks of Ma Yong near Jili Ji Bridge, were packed with people. Delicate modern women, school children wearing sachets, shop staff calling out to friends, and wealthy merchants hiring painted boats and purple-sailed vessels all chanted in unison, "Let's go watch the dragon boats." It's probably not "indulging in trivialities and losing one's ambition." To put it more elegantly, it's called encouraging enthusiasm for water sports.

There are three to five dragon boats racing together, seven to eight racing together, and more than ten racing together. As they paddle back and forth, endless supplies of wine, meat, and trophies are awarded, giving many people something to eat and something to take home. In front of the Worry-Free Temple on the Henan side, in particular, the strong swimmers exert themselves to the fullest. Even though the weather is not cooperating at noon, the light rain cannot disperse the tourists. The Haizhu Bridge is still crowded with people. Being wet on the head is like taking a shower under a cold water tap; what's the harm?

Logically, watching dragon boats beside the Worry-Free Temple should mean being carefree. Who would have thought that the old saying "extreme joy begets sorrow" would come true! At that time, more than thirty dragon boats from villages such as Dashizhuang, Litang, and Datang circled several times around the Ma Yong Bridge area. The spectators on the bridge were too enthusiastic and collapsed a part of the bridge, causing more than twenty men and women to fall into the water simultaneously. In the end, only a dozen injured people were rescued. Others, who had been greedy for the spectacle, suffered the misfortune of drowning! Qu Yuan did not endure loneliness, and gained a few comrades. This is truly a depressing event.

I Wish to Be Reborn as a Woman 193

— Bai He

Young ladies who never left their boudoirs now have their sleeves high, their heels high, and go to the office and writing room every day. They hold their chests high, competing with men for a day's dominance, and looking down their noses, they no longer put stinky men in their eyes. Women serve society, and are superior in every way, frightening each of the two hundred million men by three inches. Look, for the sake of "promoting women's careers," male employees are smashing their rice bowls in batches, suffering in silence, with no place to complain. Oppose this, and you will be scolded for not understanding the great principle of women's service in the 20th century, truly a blockhead. If you claim to be modern, unwilling to be left behind, and still stroke your gray beard, talking about women's service, then I'm sorry, you have to give your place at the table to women, there is no other way.

Neither left nor right is appropriate. In this day and age, it is difficult to be a man. "I can't do it, brother," if you can't do it as a brother, then it's better to be a sister, and someone will say "I love you." Not being a man, but being a woman, not to mention anything else, just by placing a "seeking spouse" advertisement in the newspaper, without boasting, twenty or thirty pink envelopes of considerate, tender, and affectionate responses are almost guaranteed to arrive in a day. This will truly make stinky men who post "marriage wanted" ads and receive jokes, ridicule, and sarcasm seethe with rage, with one Buddha being born and two Buddhas entering nirvana, and what about three Buddhas? It cannot be investigated.

Oh God, I am a man, this life is over, so I desperately prepare to knock through one hundred and twenty wooden fish in this life, wishing to be reborn as a woman in the next life, using several free, obligatory male servants to open doors for me, offer me seats, and add coats, offer attentiveness, and hold my pug. But I don't know if this stinky man with a face full of worry has the good fortune to transform from the Cihang Taoist into the Guanyin Bodhisattva, which makes my seventeen or eighteen buckets go up and down, making me a little uneasy.

"Big" and "Small" 194

— Yiyi Guan Zhu

As the saying goes, "Big people talk, if they say something wrong, let it pass. Little people talk, if they say something wrong, they get spanked." This describes how easy it is to be big and how difficult it is to be small. No matter where you are, as long as you are big, you will always get some advantage.

For example: in the officialdom, if you are a big official, then you can say whatever you want, even if you fart, who dares to pinch their nose and say it smells bad? Otherwise, if you are a small official like a sesame seed, then when you see your superior, you call them "Sir" in every sentence, not only must you be careful with your words, but your manners must also be impeccable. For example: in the business world, if you are a big partner, then your every move is unrestricted, and the owner entrusts you with full authority. Even if you don't speak reasonably to the employees and don't act according to human feelings, unless the junior partner is a "fool," who dares to interrupt and say "no"? Otherwise, please leave, I don't need you.

For example: in the family, if there are several brothers, if you are the "eldest brother," and if you are lucky, "your father" lives and works like a horse, earning a "family fortune," and when he passes away, "alas," "dies peacefully," then, when the brothers divide this "family fortune," of course, it is more advantageous for you to be the eldest brother, and you can get a little more. The smaller the ranking, the less you get. As for "wives," it is also more advantageous to be the big one and disadvantageous to be the small one, because the small wife has to live in a small house. Even if she gets to live with the big wife in a big mansion, then in every place, she must rely on the big wife. Otherwise, there is no way, she still has to live in a small house. As I write this, I still want to keep writing, or someone will say: Okay, let's stop, according to what you say, as long as you are big, it is always easy and advantageous. If you are small, it is always difficult and disadvantageous. Then, why is our Republic of China, a big country, being eaten by a small country like Japan? I say: this can only be attributed to fate, there is nothing to say!

Long Novel

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 195

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 8: Eloquent Words Incite the Youth to Resign and Flee;

Warm Heart Pities the Girl and Escorts the Coffin for Burial

Now that he saw him, he felt all kinds of emotions: sour, sweet, bitter, and spicy. He deliberately put on a smile and said: There is nothing else, but I have some unfortunate news to tell Madam Yang, which is that I am afraid people will say that I am relying on my brother for food, so I have already resigned from my job. Now I am taking my luggage, leaving the family, and going to the city to look for a job. Zhao Ziqiang did not know what his intention was, and felt that this person still had some ambition, so he said: Where will Mr. Gan be staying in the city? Ji Zhixin thought, it would be good to let him know his address, if he told Guizhi, and if Guizhi agreed to my proposal, he would definitely come to the city to find me. So he said: I am now a poor scholar, of course I cannot afford to stay in a hotel, and I do not want to disturb my friends, I will be staying in the Chuandong Guildhall. When Commander Zhao comes to the city, he can stop by and visit me. After speaking, he took off his hat, nodded, and left. Zhao Ziqiang did not know that he and Guizhi had developed love, and he would never have dreamed of the love triangle. He thought that he came to tell him that he had lost his job, or to beg for sympathy, but he did not know that it was a fit of pique. When it was time that day, he did not wait for the Jiang family mother and daughter to return home, and returned to the camp. The second time he came back was three days later. As soon as he entered the door, he met Madam Jiang in the front yard. After greeting her, he told her: Mr. Gan of the opposite house came here last time to bid farewell. He lost his job, did you know? Madam Jiang smiled and said: We are just ordinary neighbors, we don't have any dealings, his job is lost. As she spoke, she looked Zhao Ziqiang up and down. In her heart, she was thinking, why do you want to report such news to us? Probably Mr. Gan lost his job, and he is very proud in his heart. Madam Jiang thought so in her heart, but she did not tell Guizhi. She thought that Guizhi knew everything about Mr. Gan's every move. This time, let's not reveal it and see if Guizhi knows or not.
